                 <!-- Body -->
                 <div class="j-comment-body-container p-comment-body forum-post-body-content">
                  <!-- Content -->
                  <div class="j-comment-body forum-post-body u-typography-format text" id="forum-post-body-1" itemprop="text">
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <span style="font-size:x-large">
                      <span id="Top">
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-size:xx-large">
                       [TUTORIAL] Command Blocks
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </strong>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-size:medium">
                    Hey Guys!
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   This is a collaboration put together by the community and myself, to help you learn about how command blocks work. This topic contains designs that you'd be able to use with your custom maps, from survival islands to mini-games.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-size:x-large">
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      <u>
                       Read This Before Posting!
                      </u>
                     </strong>
                    </font>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   Before posting, please take into account that this is
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    NOT
                   </strong>
                   a tutorial for mods, textures or third-party programs. Command Blocks can't do everything, and neither can Minecraft, so if it can't be done, that's that! Well, hope this helps you, and don't forget to leave feedback!
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     NOTE:
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    In some cases, you may want to do some altering of the designs shown here. Not everyone wants the player to hit a button or walk over a pressure plate. Scroll to the bottom of this post and head over to the Minecraft Wiki to find out more!
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#f00">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     Want to help? I'm currently looking for tutorials on /summon, /setblock, dataTags, and other commands and mechanisms you do not see here. Feel free to post them!
                    </strong>
                   </font>

                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <em class="bbc">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Base Commands
                      </font>
                     </em>
                    </strong>
                   </span>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      List of commands for use on the Command Block
                     </strong>
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /testfor
                    </font>
                    ~ Tests if a player/s has a certain item, is in a certain area, or has a specific amount of Experience Orbs/Levels or Score.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /clear
                    </font>
                    ~ Is used to clear a players inventory, or to remove ALL of one item.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /difficulty
                    </font>
                    ~ Changes the difficulty to that of which is specified after the initial command.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /effect
                    </font>
                    ~ Adds an certain effect to a player for a specified amount of time.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /enchant
                    </font>
                    ~ Enchants the item the player/s is/are currently holding.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /gamemode
                    </font>
                    ~ Changes the player/s to the specified gamemode.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /gamerule
                    </font>
                    ~ Changes the gamerule specified to either true or false.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     give
                    </font>
                    ~ Gives a player/s a certain item.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /say
                    </font>
                    ~ Broadcasts the message displayed in the Command Block. Player arguements (@a,@p,@r) can beused to display a name in the broadcast.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /scoreboard
                    </font>
                    ~ Uses arguements from the Scoreboard.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /spawnpoint
                    </font>
                    ~ Sets the spawnpoint at the current location. If followed by X Y Z coordinates, this will set the player/s at a certain block.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /time
                    </font>
                    ~ Argument "set" (
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /time set
                    </font>
                    )
                    <em class="bbc">
                     number
                    </em>
                    | day | night&gt; .
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /toggledownfall
                    </font>
                    ~ Toggles rain/snow.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /tp @# x y z
                    </font>
                    ~ Teleports specified player/s to a set of X Y Z coordinates.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /weather  [
                     <em class="bbc">
                      seconds
                     </em>
                     ]
                    </font>
                    ~ Used to change the weather, and set it's duration.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /xp
                     <em class="bbc">
                      amount
                     </em>
                     &gt; [
                     <em class="bbc">
                      playername
                     </em>
                     ]
                    </font>
                    ~ Gives the player/s a specified number of Experience Orbs.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /xp
                     <em class="bbc">
                      amount
                     </em>
                     &gt;L [
                     <em class="bbc">
                      playername
                     </em>
                     ]
                    </font>
                    ~ Gives the player/s a specified number of Experience Levels.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /playsound &lt;FileLocation&gt; &lt;player&gt; [x] [y] [z] [volume] [pitch] [minimum_volume]
                    </font>
                    ~ Plays a specific sound
                    <br/>
                    according to the arguments set.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="font-size:small">
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                        /summon &lt;EntityName&gt; [x] [y] [z] [dataTag]
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                    ~ Summons an entity specific to the variables displayed. (LOOKING FOR TUTORIAL + DATATAGS)
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <span style="font-size:medium">
                     <span id="1">
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     <span style="font-size:large">
                      <strong class="bbc">
                       Command Basics
                      </strong>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <u>
                     <em class="bbc">
                      Targeting players:
                     </em>
                    </u>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     @p = Closest Player
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     @a = All Players
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     @r = Random Player
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <u>
                     <em class="bbc">
                      Game Rules
                     </em>
                    </u>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#40e0d0">
                      commandBlockOutput
                     </font>
                     - Enables/disables text output of command block commands to console.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#40e0d0">
                      doFireTick
                     </font>
                     - Enables/disables fire spread.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#40e0d0">
                      doMobLoot
                     </font>
                     - Enables/disables mob drops.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#40e0d0">
                      doMobSpawning
                     </font>
                     - Enables/disables the spawning of mobs unless you want them to ex: eggs and mob spawners will still spawn mobs
                    </em>
                    .
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#40e0d0">
                      doTileDrops
                     </font>
                     - Enables/disables blocks dropping items when broken (includes TNT destroying blocks)
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#40e0d0">
                      keepInventory
                     </font>
                     - Enables/disables keeping inventory on death
                    </em>
                    .
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#40e0d0">
                      mobGriefing
                     </font>
                     - Enables/disables creepers, ghasts, and Wither blowing up blocks, endermen picking up blocks
                    </em>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     and zombies breaking doors
                    </em>
                    .
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#40e0d0">
                      naturalRegeneration
                     </font>
                     - Allows/Disallows player to naturally regenerate health (if their hunger bar is high enough)
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     Type
                     <font style="color:#f00">
                      /gamerule
                     </font>
                    </em>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     to change the selected game rule.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <u>
                     <em class="bbc">
                      Scoreboard:
                     </em>
                    </u>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     Display Slots:
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#00f">
                      list
                     </font>
                     - Lists the players killcount in the (TAB) menu.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#00f">
                      sidebar
                     </font>
                     - Shows the players killcount on a scoreboard on the right side of the screen.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#00f">
                      belowname
                     </font>
                     - Lists the players killcount below their name label.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     Criteria:
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#008000">
                      dummy
                     </font>
                     - Score is only changed by commands, and not by game events such as death. This is useful for event flags, state mappings, and currencies.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#008000">
                      deathCount
                     </font>
                     - Counts the number of times a player has died.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#008000">
                      playerKillCount
                     </font>
                     - Counts how many PLAYER kills a player has obtained.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#008000">
                      totalKillCount
                     </font>
                     - Counts the TOTAL number of kills a player has obtained.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#008000">
                      health
                     </font>
                     - Counts how much health a player has left.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     Arguments:
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#800080">
                      score_NAME=#
                     </font>
                     - Maximum experience level for the player
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     <em class="bbc">
                      score_NAME_min
                     </em>
                     =#
                    </font>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     - Minimum experience level for the player
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <u>
                     <em class="bbc">
                      Targeting Arguments:
                     </em>
                    </u>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     x=# - X-coordinate
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     y=# - Y-coordinate
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     z=#
                    </em>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     -
                    </em>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     Z-coordinate
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     r=# - Maximum search radius
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     rm=# - Minimum search radiu
                    </em>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     s
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     c=# - Number of players. If negative, uses players from the end of the list first. When outputting through a comparator, the signal strength is equal to the number of players it locates
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     team=? - Targets players in that specific team
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     m=# - Targets players in that specific gamemode
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     name=? - Checks for players with this name. Inserting an '!' before the name checks only for players who do not have this name
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     Example:
                     <font style="color:#f00">
                      /tp @p[r=10,team=Black,m=2] 23 64 53
                     </font>
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     This would cause the
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      CLOSEST PLAYER (@p)
                     </strong>
                     on the
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      BLACK TEAM (team=Black)
                     </strong>
                     , within a
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      10 BLOCK RADIUS (r=10),
                     </strong>
                     and the
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      ADVENTURE GAMEMODE (m=2)
                     </strong>
                     to be
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      TELEPORTED (tp)
                     </strong>
                     to the coordinates 23 64 53.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     I
                    </em>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     n another situation:
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#f00">
                      /tp @a[x=23,y=64,z=53,r=20,m=1,team=Black] 32 98 13
                     </font>
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     In this case,
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      ALL PLAYERS (@a)
                     </strong>
                     on the
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      BLACK TEAM (team=Black)
                     </strong>
                     within a
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      20 BLOCK RADIUS (r=20)
                     </strong>
                     of the coordinates 23 64 53 and in the
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      GAMEMODE CREATIVE (m=1)
                     </strong>
                     would be
                    </em>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      TELEPORTED (tp)
                     </strong>
                     to the coordinates 32 98 13.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <u>
                     <em class="bbc">
                      Other:
                     </em>
                    </u>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#0f0">
                      l=#
                     </font>
                     - Maximum number of experience levels for the player
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#0f0">
                      lm=#
                     </font>
                     - Minimum number of experience levels for the player
                    </em>
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <span style="font-size:large">
                      <span id="2">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Broadcasting Messages across the world and to individuals
                      </em>
                     </span>
                    </strong>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare_104
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    World Messages
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block: /say Message Here.
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    Broadcasts a world-wide message.Player Messages
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block: /tell @p Message Here.
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    Sends the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     CLOSEST PLAYER (@p)
                    </strong>
                    a message.
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <span style="font-size:large">
                      <span id="3">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Spawnpoint
                      </em>
                     </span>
                    </strong>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare_104
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <span style="font-size:medium">
                      As you probably know, using /spawnpoint makes a wide-based spawn.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    Instead, use the command
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /spawnpoint
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     x y z
                    </font>
                    and it will pinpoint the spawn. If this doesn't work, run it through a command block on a loop. This is used for individual players, per world. You can add player variables in this manner:
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /spawnpoint @a
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     x y z.
                    </font>
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      <span id="4">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Giving Items
                      </em>
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#006400">
                      <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                       Fear
                      </a>
                      <u>
                       e
                      </u>
                      &amp;
                      <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/2741944-flazeofages/" target="">
                       FlazeOfAges
                      </a>
                     </font>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block: /give @p 267
                    </font>
                    This will give the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     CLOSEST
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     (@p)
                    </strong>
                    player an
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     IRON SWORD (267).
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      NOTE:
                     </strong>
                    </em>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     Item ID and player variable will change based on your map.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      FlazeOfAges In-depth Tutorial:
                     </strong>
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#282828">
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="font-size:small">
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                        For many versions mapmakers had to use dispensers and large amounts of redstone wiring to give a player equipment. Minecraft 1.4.2 changed everything.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#282828">
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="font-size:small">
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                        /give works on a few basic arguments: Who you give the item to, what the item is, how many of the item to give, what damage value the item has and further datatags. Like this:
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     /
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     give
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#080">
                     &lt;player&gt;
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     ID
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     &gt;
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     [
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     quantity
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     ]
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     [
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     damage value
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     ]
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     [
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     dataTag
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     ]
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#282828">
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="font-size:small">
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                        Let's start simple:
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     /
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     give
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     @p
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     minecraft
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     stone
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     1
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     0
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#282828">
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="font-size:small">
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                        This will give the closest player one stone block. You don't have to target the closest player, @a will give ALL players one stone, @r will give a RANDOM player one stone. The next bit says "minecraft:stone" since a recent update you no longer have to use the numerical id's for items/blocks and it has been stated that numerical id's will not be supported in the future. For a list of items and their values, go
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                    <a href="http://minecraft.gamepedia.com/Data_values" target="">
                     HERE
                    </a>
                    <font style="color:#282828">
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="font-size:small">
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                        . Following that is the item count, you can make this number as large as you like. After the count is the damage value, some items aren't affected by damage values while others depend on it. Here's another /give example.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     give
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     @p
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     minecraft
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     potion
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     64
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     16428
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#282828">
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="font-size:small">
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                        This command will give you a stack of "Splash potion of Harming". Potions are one of the most common items to be associated with damage values. For a more in-depth tutorial on custom potions, go
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                    <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/topic/2222857-tutorial-custom-potions/" target="">
                     HERE
                    </a>
                    <font style="color:#282828">
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="font-size:small">
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                        .
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#282828">
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="font-size:small">
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                        Following the damage value is where mapmakers/redstoners shine, data tags. I won't go into those too much other than give an example of what you can do with them.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     give
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     @p
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     279
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     1
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     0
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     {
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     display
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :{
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#606">
                     Name
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#606">
                     Destroyer
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     ,
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#606">
                     Lore
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :[
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     I am
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#606">
                     Tank
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     !
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#606">
                     Conqueror
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     of
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#606">
                     Worlds
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     ]},
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     ench
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :[{
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     id
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     16
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     ,
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     lvl
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     2
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     },{
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     id
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     17
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     ,
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     lvl
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     5
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     },{
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     id
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     18
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     ,
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     lvl
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     5
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     },{
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     id
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     34
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     ,
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#000">
                     lvl
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     10
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     }],
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#606">
                     AttributeModifiers
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :[{
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#606">
                     Operation
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     0
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     ,
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#606">
                     UUIDLeast
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     1
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     ,
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#606">
                     UUIDMost
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     :
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#066">
                     1
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">

                    </font>

                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">

                    </font>

                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">

                    </font>

                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">

                    </font>

                    </font>

                    </font>
