                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#660">
                     }]}
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <span style="font-size:large">
                      <span id="5">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Giving Potions
                      </em>
                     </span>
                    </strong>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare_104
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <span style="font-size:medium">
                      <font style="color:#f00">
                       Command: /give @p 373 1
                      </font>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     8259
                    </font>
                    This will give the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     CLOSEST PLAYER (@p)
                    </strong>
                    one
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     POTION OF FIRE RESISTANCE (8259)
                    </strong>
                    lasting 8 minutes. The Potion ID is 373, but the Potion DV is always different.As you can see, the ID comes first, then the quantity, then the DV.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftwiki.net/wiki/Potions" target="">
                      The Potion DV list can be found here on the Minecraft Wiki!
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      <span id="6">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Giving Enchanted Items
                      </em>
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <em class="bbc">
                     The player MUST be holding the item they are going to enchant. This means selecting the first FREE slot on their equipment bar.
                    </em>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block One: /give @p
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     267
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    Gives the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     NEAREST PLAYER (@p)
                    </strong>
                    an
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     IRON SWORD (267).
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block Two: /enchant @p 16 2
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    Enchants the item the nearest player is holding. In this case, it would give a sword Sharpness II enchantment.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <a href="http://www.minecraftwiki.net/wiki/Enchanting" target="">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      More on Enchantments can be found here on the Minecraft Wiki!
                     </strong>
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      <span id="7">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Potion Effects
                      </em>
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <em class="bbc">
                     Using Nausea as an example.
                    </em>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block One:
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     effect @p 9 30
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    This will cause the player to have
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     NAUSEA (9)
                    </strong>
                    of
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     30 SECONDS (30).
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <a href="http://www.minecraftwiki.net/wiki/Potion_effects" target="">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      More on Potion Effects can be found here on the Minecraft Wiki!
                     </strong>
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <span style="font-size:large">
                      <span id="8">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Weather
                      </em>
                     </span>
                    </strong>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <span style="font-size:medium">
                     <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                     </div>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <span style="font-size:medium">
                     To toggle the weather between Snow, Rain and Shine, use the following command.
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <span style="font-size:medium">
                     <font style="color:#f00">
                      Command:
                     </font>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <font style="color:#f00">
                    /weather  [duration]
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <span style="font-size:large">
                      <span id="9">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Teleportation
                      </em>
                     </span>
                     <em class="bbc">
                      <span style="font-size:large">
                       To Set Coordinates
                      </span>
                     </em>
                    </strong>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block: /tp @p
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     x y z
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     The variables coloured in
                     <font style="color:#800080">
                      Purple
                     </font>
                     are the coordinates, and will be different for everyone.
                    </em>
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      <span id="10">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Relative Teleportation
                      </em>
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#006400">
                      ~
                     </font>
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/475017-astrospud/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       AstroSpud
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <em class="bbc">
                     This command teleports you a number of blocks away from your current location.
                    </em>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block: /tp @p ~
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     x
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     y
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     z
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     The variables coloured in
                     <font style="color:#800080">
                      Purple
                     </font>
                     indicate how far the player will travel along each axis.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     Example:
                    </em>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block:
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /tp @p ~5 ~10 ~15
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    This command will
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     TELEPORT (tp)
                    </strong>
                    the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     CLOSEST PLAYER (@p)
                    </strong>
                    5 block along the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     X axis (sideways)
                    </strong>
                    , 10 blocks along the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     Y axis (up/down)
                    </strong>
                    and 15 blocks along the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     Z axis (front/back)
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     .
                    </strong>
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      <span id="11">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Experience Shops
                      </em>
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <em class="bbc">
                     You can change the item by using a different Item ID. Google search it.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Lower Command Block: /give @p[lm=5] 267
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    This will give the nearest player an
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     IRON SWORD (267)
                    </strong>
                    for a
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     MINIMUM (lm)
                    </strong>
                    of
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     5 EXPERIENCE LEVELS (=5)
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Upper Command Block: /xp -5L @p[lm=5]
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    This will
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     SUBTRACT
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     5 EXPERI
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     ENCE LEVELS (-5L)
                    </strong>
                    from the nearest player, if that player has a
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     MINIMUM (lm)
                    </strong>
                    of
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     5 EXPERIENCE LEVELS
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     (=5)
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     .
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    When giving potions, you must use the command like this:
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block: /give @p[lm=5] 373 3 16373
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    This would give the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     CLOSEST PLAYER (@p)
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     3 (3) POTIONS (373)
                    </strong>
                    of
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     INSTANT HEALTH (16373).
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    The Potion ID comes first, then the amount, then the Potion value.
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      <span id="12">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Scoreboard
                      </em>
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <em class="bbc">
                     This can be done as a regular command
                    </em>
                    .
                    <em class="bbc">
                     Not compatible with Bukkit servers.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    Type
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /scoreboard objectives add
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     Points
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#008000">
                     totalKillCount
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     Points
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    Next, type
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /scoreboard objectives
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     setdisplay
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#00f">
                     sidebar
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     Points
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      Note:
                     </strong>
                     The words coloured in
                     <font style="color:#800080">
                      Purple
                     </font>
                     can be whatever you wish them to be, just make sure they are the same in both commands.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    Now, when you kill something, or someone, your kill count will show on a sidebar to the right side of the screen.
                    <br/>
                    The argument "sidebar" can be changed to any of the following:
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#00f">
                     list
                    </font>
                    - Lists the players killcount in the (TAB) menu.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#00f">
                     sidebar
                    </font>
                    - Shows the players killcount on a scoreboard on the right side of the screen.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#00f">
                     belowname
                    </font>
                    - Lists the players killcount below their name label.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    The argument "totalKillCount" can be changed to any of the following, depending on your purposes:
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#008000">
                     dummy
                    </font>
                    - Score is only changed by commands, and not by game events such as death. This is useful for event flags, state mappings, and currencies.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#008000">
                     deathCount
                    </font>
                    - Counts the number of times a player has died.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#008000">
                     playerKillCount
                    </font>
                    - Counts how many PLAYER kills a player has obtained.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#008000">
                     totalKillCount
                    </font>
                    - Count the TOTAL number of kills a player has obtained.
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#008000">
                     health
                    </font>
                    - Counts how much health a player has left.
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      <span id="13">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Point Shops (Using points from the Scoreboard)
                      </em>
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <em class="bbc">
                     Scoreboard must be activated for this to work!
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Lower Command Block Command: /scoreboard players remove @p[score_
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     Points
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     _min=5]
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     Points
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     5
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    This will
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     SUBTRACT 5 POINTS (remove Points 5)
                    </strong>
                    from the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     CLOSEST PLAYER
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     (@p)
                    </strong>
                    if the player has a
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     MINIMUM (score_Points_min)
                    </strong>
                    of
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     5 Points
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     .
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Upper Command Block Command: /give @p[score_
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     Points
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     _min=5]
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     267
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    This will give the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     CLOSEST PLAYER (@p)
                    </strong>
                    an
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     IRON SWORD (267)
                    </strong>
                    if the player has a
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     MINIMUM (score_Points_min)
                    </strong>
                    of
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     5 Points.
                    </strong>
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <font style="color:#006400">
                      <span id="14">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Having NPCs speak accordingly
                      </em>
                     </font>
                    </span>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#006400">
                      <span style="font-size:large">
                       - Gender
                      </span>
                     </font>
                    </em>
                   </strong>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#006400">
                      ~
                     </font>
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/56929-raecchi/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Raecchi
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    Giving your character a gender:STEP ONE:
                    <img alt="" height="" src="http://i.imgur.com/kjOV4wc.png" width=""/>
                    STEP TWO:
                    <img alt="" height="" src="http://i.imgur.com/r4SnaZt.png" width=""/>
                   </div>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      <span id="15">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       How to make doors that cost experience levels to open
                      </em>
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    <em class="bbc">
                     When making this, make sure you do not have any experience levels. Same goes for resetting the system.
                    </em>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block One: /testfor @p[lm=5]
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    This will run a
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     TEST (testfor)
                    </strong>
                    on the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     CLOSEST PLAYER (@p)
                    </strong>
                    to see if they have a
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     MINIMUM LEVEL (lm)
                    </strong>
                    of
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     5
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     EXPERIENCE LEVELS.
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    Behind this command block, place a redstone comparator. If the player tests positive (meaning the player has a minimum of 5 xp levels) the command block will output a signal to the comparator.
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     MAKE SURE THE COMPARATOR IS NOT IN SUBTRACTION MODE.
                    </strong>
                    Have this comparator facing another command block.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block Two (with this comparator):
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /tp @p[lm=5
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     ]
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     x y z
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    If the player tests positive to what we did earlier, the player will be teleported to our coordinates and activate a pressure plate. That pressure plate will activate a signal and do the following:
                    <ol>
                     <li>
                      <font style="color:#f00">
                       /xp -5L @p[lm=5]
                      </font>
                     </li>
                    </ol>
                    Player has
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     5 EXPERIENCE LEVELS TAKEN FROM THEM (-5L)
                    </strong>
                    if player has a
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     MINIMUM OF 5 LEVELS (lm=5)
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    2.
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /say Door Opened!
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    Broadcasts a message across the map telling all players that a door has been opened.
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    3.
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /tp @p
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     x y z
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    This will teleport the
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     CLOSEST PLAYER (@p)
                    </strong>
                    to the coordinates of your choice. I suggest teleporting the player to a block in front of the button.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Also, for the door, when the player teleports to the coordinates of the pressure plate, run a wire to an inverter to switch it off. This will deactivate a redstone torch, and make the pistons retract, releasing sand. This means the door has fallen, and is open.
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     If you don't want to use sand, you can use an Iron door and wire the pressure plate up to a T-Flip Flop, which will be wired up to the door.
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    Coming off the same line of redstone we were first using, make a new section.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     Command Block One: /testfor @p[l=4]
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    This will run a
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     TEST (testfor)
                    </strong>
                    to see if the player has a
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     MAXIMUM (l)
                    </strong>
                    of
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     4 EXPERIENCE LEVELS.
                    </strong>
                    This means the player has 4 levels or LESS. If the player tests positive to this test, he has tested negative to the other.
                    <br/>
                    Now, to show the player he doesn't have enough xp, we will do the following:
                    <br/>
                    Place down a redstone comparator branching off the command block, then place another command block in front of the comparator.
                    <br/>
                    Have it run this message:
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /tell @p You do not have the required amount of funds to perform that action.
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    If this message appears, the player needs more XP to open the door.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     The above can also be done with points from the scoreboard. Just change the
                     <font style="color:#f00">
                      @p[lm=5]
                     </font>
                     to
                     <font style="color:#f00">
                      @p[score_
                     </font>
                     <font style="color:#800080">
                      Points
                     </font>
                     <font style="color:#f00">
                      _min]
                     </font>
                     and the
                     <font style="color:#f00">
                      @p[l=4
                     </font>
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#f00">
                      ]
                     </font>
                     to
                     <font style="color:#f00">
                      @p[score_
                     </font>
                     <font style="color:#800080">
                      Points
                     </font>
                     <font style="color:#f00">
                      =4]
                     </font>
                    </strong>
                   </div>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <span style="font-size:large">
                      <span id="16">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Week Counter
                      </em>
                     </span>
                    </strong>
                   </font>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     ~
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/56929-raecchi/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Raecchi
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <span style="font-size:medium">
                     <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                     </div>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   Something I designed for a map I'm working on; thought I should share it so other people could use the same idea.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    Step one:
                   </strong>
                   <em class="bbc">
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    /scoreboard objectives add week dummy Week
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    /scoreboard objectives add showweek dummy Week
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    /scoreboard objectives setdisplay sidebar showweek
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    Step Two:
                   </strong>
                   <br/>
                   Build this:
                   <img alt="" height="" src="http://i.imgur.com/cwzgpsW.png" width=""/>
                   And now you have a working setup to count and display a week, which can easily be adjusted for shorter/longer spans of time.Possible uses:(All using a testfor command block somewhere)
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     Wire to redstone lamps around a spawner to make rare, specific day spawns
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     Have shops that are only open on certain days of the week
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     Hook up noteblocks for Sunday church chimes
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     Use as part of a countdown for time-limited maps
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     Make some kind of Groundhog Day/Majora's Mask scenario
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     If you count weeks, you could even set up Minecraft months and years!
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <br/>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    <span style="font-size:large">
                     <font style="color:#006400">
                      <span id="17">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       Experience Bank
                      </em>
                     </font>
                    </span>
                   </strong>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <span style="font-size:medium">
                     <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                     </div>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    Used to store and withdraw experience levels in a Bank.
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   Command:
                   <font style="color:#f00">
                    /scoreboard objectives add Money dummy Money
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   Next:
                   <font style="color:#f00">
                    /scoreboard objectives setdisplay list Money
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   Okay, let's dive into the command blocks! We'll start with the "Deposit" section.
                   <img alt="" height="" src="http://i.imgur.com/kyKu3Fq.png" width=""/>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    ^^ This will make the player teleport to a pressure plate at the set coordinates to deposit ^^
                   </strong>
                   <img alt="" height="" src="http://i.imgur.com/mCnDWd0.png" width=""/>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    ^^ The layout I am using ^^
                   </strong>
                   <img alt="" height="" src="http://i.imgur.com/Kam5Ap0.png" width=""/>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    ^^ This will remove 5 experience levels from the player when they deposit ^^
                   </strong>
                   <img alt="" height="" src="http://i.imgur.com/uNmBVAU.png" width=""/>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    ^^ This will convert the 5 experience levels into a dummy score, which can be found in the [TAB] menu ^^
                   </strong>
                   <img alt="" height="" src="http://i.imgur.com/iXF2b5y.png" width=""/>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    ^^ This will teleport the player back to the Bank lobby
                   </strong>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    ^^
                   </strong>
                   <img alt="" height="" src="http://i.imgur.com/fw2X7YE.png" width=""/>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    -- Withdraw Segment Currently Out Of Order --
                   </strong>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#006400">
                      <span id="18">
                      </span>
                      <em class="bbc">
                       "Rounds" System
                      </em>
                     </font>
                    </strong>
                   </span>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     ~
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/512987-feare-104/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Feare
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     and
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/56929-raecchi/" target="">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                       Raecchi
                      </font>
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    Firstly, you want to run the following commands
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     in order:
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    1.
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /scoreboard objectives add Rounds dummy Rounds:
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    2.
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /scoreboard objectives add showRounds
                    </font>
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     dummy Rounds
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    3.
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /scoreboard objectives setdisplay sidebar showRounds
                    </font>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    Next, download the elevator. I'll post a MCEdit schematic at the bottom of this tutorial.
                    <br/>
                    Enjoy!

                         <em class="bbc">
                          The "Mystery Box"
                         </em>

                           Feare
                          </font>
                         </a>
                        </strong>

                     Preliminary:
                    </strong>
                   </font>

                    </em>

                   </font>

                      section if you need any help!
