                   <br/>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#006400">
                     <em class="bbc">
                      <span style="font-size:large">
                       <span style="font-family:arial,helvetica,sans-serif">
                        <span id="20">
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <strong class="bbc">
                        <span style="font-size:large">
                         <em class="bbc">
                          Playsound
                         </em>
                        </span>
                       </strong>
                      </span>
                     </em>
                    </font>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <span style="font-size:medium">
                      <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/308222-minihilly/" target="">
                       <font style="color:#006400">
                        ~minihilly
                       </font>
                      </a>
                     </span>
                     <font style="color:#006400">
                      <em class="bbc">
                      </em>
                     </font>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     <em class="bbc">
                      <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                      </div>
                     </em>
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     Playsound:
                    </strong>
                   </em>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <font style="color:#f00">
                     /playsound &lt;FileLocation&gt; &lt;player&gt; [x] [y] [z] [volume] [pitch] [minimum_volume]
                    </font>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    Whereas [] are optional, locate the sounds at
                    <em class="bbc">
                     .minecraft\assets\sound\
                    </em>
                    , and name them after the location within the sound folder; so .minecraft\assets\sound\
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     mob\pig\say
                    </strong>
                    will become
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     mob.pig.say
                    </strong>
                    - it is IMPORTANT to note that numbers (0-9) CANNOT be used when referring to sound files; instead, the command will cycle through numbered files randomly (e.g. say1, say2, say3 will get picked randomly using the referrer mob.pig.say).
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <em class="bbc">
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     [x] [y] [z]
                    </strong>
                    coords are NOT referrers for the player's position, they a the set co-ords for where the sound plays from; for example, setting this to
                    <em class="bbc">
                     0 2 3
                    </em>
                    will play a sound at x0, y2, and z3.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     [volume]
                    </strong>
                    specifies the volume of the sound played (I think the maximum is 10
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     *
                    </strong>
                    )
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     [Pitch]
                    </strong>
                    Specifies the Pitch (e.g. 1 will increase it by one octave, -1 will decrease it; decimals are accepted). I'm not sure, but I think the maximum value might be 6
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     *
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     [minimum_volume]
                    </strong>
                    specify a minimum volume value - I think this means that, if the player is distant from the sound, how quietly it will reach before cutting out (essentially acting as a radius for the sound), but it doesn't appear to work
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     *
                    </strong>
                    <strong class="bbc">
                     *
                    </strong>
                    Denotes uncertainty, or required confirmation.
                    <strong class="bbc">
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <font style="color:#006400">
                      <em class="bbc">
                       <span style="font-size:large">
                        <span style="font-family:arial, helvetica, sans-serif">
                         <span id="21">
                          Custom Potions ~
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </em>
                     </font>
                    </em>
                    <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/user/2741944-flazeofages/" target="">
                     <font style="color:#006400">
                      <span style="font-size:large">
                       <span style="font-family:arial, helvetica, sans-serif">
                        F
                        <strong class="bbc">
                         <span style="font-size:medium">
                          <u>
                           lazeOfAges
                          </u>
                         </span>
                        </strong>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </font>
                    </a>
                    <em class="bbc">
                     <strong class="bbc">
                      <font style="color:#006400">
                      </font>
                     </strong>
                    </em>
                   </em>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                         To give any item/block we would use:
                        </div>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#232323">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         /
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                         give
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         @p
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        The item id for a potion is 373, so we would use:
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#232323">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         /
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                         give
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         @p
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         373
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         1
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        This gives a basic potion (
                        <font style="color:#090">
                         <u>
                          water bottle
                         </u>
                        </font>
                        ) with the count of one (that come from the '1' place after '373'). So we now have a water bottle but what if we want it to give some actual effects? To do that we have to add one more number after our count, this number is known as the 'damage' of the potion. Changing the damage of a potion will give different effects, so what happens if we give our water bottle a damage of 1?
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#232323">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         /
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                         give
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         @p
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         373
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         1
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         1
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        See that? We just got a basic Potion of Regeneration. We can use this
                        <font style="color:#090">
                         <u>
                          damage
                         </u>
                        </font>
                        value system to create all kinds of potions. For example, a damage of 2 will give a Potion of Swiftness etc.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        This is all well and good, but we don't have any "custom" potions yet. We can add custom potion effects by changing the potion's DataTag. This is achieved through the use of 'CustomPotionEffects'.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#232323">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         /
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                         give
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         @p
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         373
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         1
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         1
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         {
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#606">
                         CustomPotionEffects
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         :[{
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#606">
                         Id
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         :
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         2
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         ,
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#606">
                         Amplifier
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         :
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         1
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         ,
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#606">
                         Duration
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         :
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         200
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         }]}
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        Woah, slow down there! Let's break this up:
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#232323">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        <font style="color:#080">
                         "CustomPotionEffects:"
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#008000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        CustomPotionEffects
                       </span>
                       is what is telling the command that we want to add custom effect to the potion.
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        <font style="color:#232323">
                         <font style="color:#080">
                          "Id:2"
                         </font>
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        The id is specifying what effect we want. In this case, ID 2 is Slowness. For effect ID's visit the
                        <font style="color:#232323">
                         <strong class="bbc">
                         </strong>
                         <a href="http://minecraft.gamepedia.com/Status_effect" target="">
                          <font style="color:#042eee">
                           <strong class="bbc">
                            Minecraft Wiki
                           </strong>
                          </font>
                         </a>
                         .
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        <font style="color:#232323">
                         <font style="color:#080">
                          "Amplifier:1"
                         </font>
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        The amplifier is enhancing our potion from basic Slowness I. Keep in mind that an amplifier of 0 is considered Slowness I, so an amplifier of 1 gives us Slowness II.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        <font style="color:#232323">
                         <font style="color:#080">
                          "Duration:200"
                         </font>
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        The duration is telling our potion how long to apply the effect.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <strong class="bbc">
                        IMPORTANT:
                       </strong>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        Duration is measured in ticks (there a 20 ticks per second) so this potion gives a duration of 10 seconds.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#008000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       So when we put everything together, we get a Slowness II potion with a duration of 10 seconds.
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    {
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    CustomPotionEffects
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :[{
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Id
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    2
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ,
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Amplifier
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    1
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ,
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Duration
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    200
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    }]}
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#018000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        That's all well and good, but what if we want multiple effects on our potion? That's simple enough, all we have to do is add another set of data after what we had previously entered.
                        <font style="color:#232323">
                         <strong class="bbc">
                          IMPORTANT:
                         </strong>
                        </font>
                        Be sure to seperate your effects with a comma, like shown below.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#232323">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         /
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                         give
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         @p
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         373
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         1
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         1
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#000">
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         {
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#606">
                         CustomPotionEffects
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         :[{
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#606">
                         Id
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         :
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         2
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         ,
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#606">
                         Amplifier
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         :
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         1
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         ,
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#606">
                         Duration
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         :
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         200
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         },{
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#606">
                         Id
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         :
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#066">
                         9
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         ,
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#606">
                         Amplifier
                        </font>
                        <font style="color:#660">
                         :
                        </font>
                        3
                       </span>
                       ,
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <span style="font-size:x-small">
                    <font style="color:#800080">
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       Duration
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                   </span>
                   <font style="color:#232323">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-size:x-small">
                        :
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <span style="font-size:x-small">
                    <font style="color:#008080">
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       200
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </font>
                   </span>
                   <font style="color:#232323">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       }]}
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#008000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        This potion now gives us Slowness II and Nausea for 10 seconds.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        But we want a more interesting name than "Potion of Slowness", to achieve this we can add a custom name to our potion using the
                        <u>
                         display tag
                        </u>
                        .
                        <strong class="bbc">
                         IMPORTANT:
                        </strong>
                        Be sure to lay this out exactly as below, or it will not work.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                      <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                       {
                       <font style="color:#800080">
                        display:
                       </font>
                       {
                       <font style="color:#800080">
                        Name:
                       </font>
                       <font style="color:#008080">
                        Potion of Lead Feet
                       </font>
                       }}
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#008000">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                        We can now place our custom name into our our pre-made potion as shown below.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                      <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                       /give 373 1 1 {display:{Name:Potion of Lead Feet},CustomPotionEffects:{Id:2, Amplifier:1,Duration:200},{Id:9,Amplifier:0,Duration:200}]}
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                      <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                       <font style="color:#f00">
                        <span style="font-family:Georgia">
                         <span style="font-size:large">
                          Voil!
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </font>
                       We now have a fully custom potion with a custom name.
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                      <span style="font-family:Helvetica Neue">
                       To learn more about DataTags and how they work, head over to minihilly's post
                       <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/topic/1969520-17-using-summon-give-datatags-in-map-making-tutorials/" target="">
                        HERE
                       </a>
                       .
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <span id="22">
                     <font style="color:#006400">
                      Setblock
                     </font>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    </div>
                   </span>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                      Using
                      <font style="color:#f00">
                       /setblock:
                      </font>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                       As of 1.7.2, Mojang implemented a feature into mine craft that would forever change the way mapmakers view blocks, /setblock. The setblock command essentially allows a command block (or player) to
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span style="background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255)">
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#f00">
                    <u>
                     <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                      <span style="font-size:small">
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                        remotely
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255)">
                     </span>
                    </u>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#006400">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                       place blocks into the world. Here's the syntax:
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#f00">
                    /setblock x y z &lt;BlockID&gt; data-method dataTag
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                      Start your command with /setblock followed by the coordinates of where the block should be placed. After the coordinates goes the alphabetical ID of the block being placed (NOTE: Future versions of mine craft will not support numerical ID's, so for a full list of alphabetical ID's, go
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <a href="http://minecraft.gamepedia.com/Data_values#Block_IDs" target="">
                    <u>
                     HERE
                    </u>
                   </a>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                      .). Following the block ID is the
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <span style="background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255)">
                   </span>
                   <font style="color:#f00">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <u>
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                        block data
                       </span>
                      </u>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                      . Most blocks will have a data of 0, but some block (like wool or logs) heavily depend on data values to change their appearance. The method of which the block is placed after the data value. There are three methods available: "keep" summons the block if the space is empty, "replace" will set the specified block no matter what it formally was, and "destroy" will set the block as well as display the particles of the block being destroyed.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                      Compared to other commands, /setblock doesn't much in the way of data tags, but here are some that are worthy to note:
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   /setblock ~~1 ~minecraft:skull 1 replace {ExtraType:FireArceus64,SkullType:3,Rot:0}
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                      The above will set the block above the command block to a skull with my skin on it, you can change the name to make it anyone else's.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                      For a full list of setblock data tags, go
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <a href="http://minecraft.gamepedia.com/Chunk_format#Tile_Entity_Format" target="">
                    <u>
                     HERE
                    </u>
                   </a>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                      .
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(242, 246, 249)">
                      Ta-Daa! You have now learn't how to use /setblock. As always, here is a command that shows the full extent of /setblock:
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   ]
                   <br/>
                   /setblock ~~~minecraft:mob_spawner 0 destroy {SpawnCount:1,SpawnRange:13,RequiredPlayerRange:64,Delay:5,MinSpawnDelay:5,MaxSpawnDelay:10,MaxNearbyEntities:50,EntityId:FireworksRocketEntity,SpawnData:{LifeTime:40,FireworksItem:{id:401,Count:1,tag:{Fireworks:{Explosions:[{Flicker:1,Trail:1,Type:1,Colors:[255,16711680,16776960],FadeColors:[255,16711680,16776960]}]}}}}}
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <span id="23">
                     Summon
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-size:large">
                    <div class="spoiler" data-spoiler-title="">
                    </div>
                   </span>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                      Using /summon:
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                    <span style="font-size:small">
                     <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                      Not too long ago, there was a time when mobs had to be summoned from dispensers of custom spawners made with MC-Edit. But that all changed with the addition with /summon in 1.7.2. Let's take a look at some code.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    /
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                    summon
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    EntityName
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    &gt;
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    [
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                    x
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ]
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    [
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                    y
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ]
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    [
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                    z
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ]
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    [
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                    dataTag
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ]
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       This is the syntax for all /summon commands. Start with /summon followed by the name of the entity/mob you want to spawn E.g Pig, Sheep, PrimedTnt; for a
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#090">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <u>
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                        full list
                       </span>
                      </u>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       of entities and their names, go
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <a href="http://minecraft.gamepedia.com/Data_values#Entity_IDs" target="">
                    <u>
                     HERE
                    </u>
                   </a>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       . After the entity's name are the coordinates of the spawn.
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       Following the coordinates is were some of the more complex command block functions come in; Data Tags. I'll be covering some of the more commonly used tags, but if you want to learn more you can go
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/topic/1969520-17-using-summon-give-datatags-in-map-making-tutorials/" target="">
                    <u>
                     HERE
                    </u>
                   </a>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       or
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <a href="http://minecraft.gamepedia.com/Chunk_format" target="">
                    <u>
                     HERE
                    </u>
                   </a>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       .
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       So let's spawn a basic Pig:
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    /
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                    summon
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Pig
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ~
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ~
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    1
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ~
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       Following this is where the
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#090">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <u>
                       <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                        data tag
                       </span>
                      </u>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       goes. Let's give the pig a saddle.
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    /
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                    summon
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Pig
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ~
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ~
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    1
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ~
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    {
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Saddled
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    1
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    }
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       See what happened there? It is very important when using tags that you open and close each tag respectively. The Saddle tag is a boolean value, meaning it is either 1 or 0. What happens if we want the pig to have a custom name as well?
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    /
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                    summon
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Pig
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ~
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ~
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    1
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ~
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    {
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Saddled
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    1
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ,
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    CustomName
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#080">
                    "Piggy"
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    }
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <strong class="bbc">
                    NOTE:
                   </strong>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       We do not have to make a new set of brackets for every tag, simply separate each tag with a comma.
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#282828">
                    <span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, Tahoma, sans-serif">
                     <span style="font-size:small">
                      <span style="background-color:rgb(232, 239, 244)">
                       So there you go! Now you can use /summon to spawn entities with great ease. Before I finish, here is an example of the kind of things you can do with /summon.
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </font>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    /
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                    summon
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Skeleton
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    -
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    864
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    59
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    327
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    {
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    CustomName
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Skeletor
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ,
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    CustomNameVisible
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    1
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ,
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    SkeletonType
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    1
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ,
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Attributes
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :[{
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">

                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                    generic
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    .
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">
                    knockbackResistance
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ,
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    Base
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    1
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    },{
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">

                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">

                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">

                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#000">

                   </font>

                   </font>

                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    }],
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#606">
                    DropChances
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :[
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    0f
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ,
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    0f
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ,
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    0f
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ,
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#066">
                    0f

                   <font style="color:#066">

                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    ],
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#090">
                    <u>
                     <font style="color:#606">
                      Equipment
                     </font>
                    </u>
                   </font>
                   <font style="color:#660">
                    :[{

                 <li class="p-comment-statitem forum-title normal">

                 <li class="p-comment-statitem join-date">

                 <!-- Body -->
                 <div class="j-comment-body-container p-comment-body forum-post-body-content">
                  <!-- Content -->
                  <div class="j-comment-body forum-post-body u-typography-format text" id="forum-post-body-4" itemprop="text">
                   You forgot about relative teleportation.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   If you add a ~ before the number, it'll teleport that much in that direction. For example, /tp @p ~5 ~0~0 would send you 5 blocks forward on the x axis.
                  </div>
                  <!-- Attachments -->
                 </div>

                <!-- Comment Content -->
                <div class="p-comment-content forum-post-body-container">
                 <!-- Body -->
                 <div class="j-comment-body-container p-comment-body forum-post-body-content">
                  <!-- Content -->
                  <div class="j-comment-body forum-post-body u-typography-format text" id="forum-post-body-9" itemprop="text">
                   I think you should include targeting arguments.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   Basic targeting arguments:
                   <br/>
                   x=?:	  X-coordinate.
                   <br/>
                   y=?:	  Y-coordinate.
                   <br/>
                   z=?:	   Z-coordinate.
                   <br/>
                   r=?:	   Search radius.
                   <br/>
                   team=:   Search for players on a specific team.
                   <br/>
                   m=(0, 1 or 2):	  Game mode.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   Examples:
                   <br/>
                   tp @p[r=10,team=???] (put coordinates here) will teleport the nearest player on the ??? team that is within a radius of 10 blocks from the command block.
                   <br/>
                   gamemode 0 @a[x=23,y=64,z=53,r=20,m=!0] Will change the game mode to survival for all players within a 20 block radius of the coordinates 23 64 53, who do not already have survival.
                  </div>
                  <!-- Attachments -->
                 </div>
                </div>

                  <!-- Content -->
                  <div class="j-comment-body forum-post-body u-typography-format text" id="forum-post-body-12" itemprop="text">
                   <blockquote class="source-quote">
                    <div class="quote-content">
                     <div class="quote-body">
                      <div class="quote-source">
                       Quote from
                       <a class="quote-author" href="/comments/28049950">
                        Tiiny_BosS
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <strong class="bbc">
                       <span style="font-family:courier new, courier, monospace">
                        <font style="color:#daa520">
                         Alright I got a question. How do I give a player Potion of Resistance (373 : 8193) as when I put it into the command block like this: :
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </strong>
                      <strong class="bbc">
                       <span style="font-family:courier new, courier, monospace">
                        <font style="color:#daa520">
                         /give @a 373 : 8193 and I've also tried /give @a 373:8193
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </strong>
                      <br/>
                      <strong class="bbc">
                       <span style="font-family:courier new, courier, monospace">
                        <font style="color:#daa520">
                         BUT IT DOESN'T WORK!
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </strong>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family:courier new, courier, monospace">
                       <font style="color:#daa520">
                        <strong class="bbc">
                         Please reply as soon as possible. It's really bugging me :/
                        </strong>
                       </font>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <strong class="bbc">
                       <span style="font-family:courier new, courier, monospace">
                        <font style="color:#daa520">
                         Oh and is there a way to give an item and make it go into a specific slot??
                        </font>
                       </span>
                      </strong>
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                   </blockquote>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   You will probably have better luck giving custom items with droppers.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   What you do is create a 1x 1z 2/3y space with droppers connected to a pressure plate.
                   <br/>
                   Put your custom item(s) in the dropper(s), and have the command block teleport the player into the chamber, and have another one teleport the player back out.
                   <br/>
                   If you want items to be infinite, go into an NBT editor(I mostly use the NBT editor filter for MCedit when I do this), and change the item count value to -1.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   As for the making items go into a specific slot: Yes, with NBT editing you can do that. Check out Hypixel's Wither's Challenge map. The class select design is pretty much the solution to what you're looking for.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   Alternatively, if you want to see the design I was talking about, you can check out my map, "Conquest"
                   <a href="http://www.minecraftforum.net/topic/1757154-conquest-no-mods-required-pvp-multiplayer-map-download/" target="">
                    here
                   </a>
                   , and see how I've done it.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   Hope that helps
                   <img alt=":)" border="0" data-class="" src="http://media-minecraftforum.cursecdn.com/avatars/0/14/635356669596273706.png" title=":)"/>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <blockquote class="source-quote">
                    <div class="quote-content">
                     <div class="quote-body">
                      <div class="quote-source">
                       Quote from
                       <a class="quote-author" href="/comments/28049949">
                        Feare_104
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      I had a thought about this this morning. Once I get home from my friends place I'll update the thread.
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                   </blockquote>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   If you like, I could provide a tutorial for some commonly needed command block contraptions, like shop designs and class select systems, with screenshots.
                   <img alt=":)" border="0" data-class="" src="http://media-minecraftforum.cursecdn.com/avatars/0/14/635356669596273706.png" title=":)"/>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   By the way: This is a very good thread, Feare
                   <img alt=":)" border="0" data-class="" src="http://media-minecraftforum.cursecdn.com/avatars/0/14/635356669596273706.png" title=":)"/>

                   <br/>

                   There is no way yet to put an item into a specific slot, unless you use a different program, as Benjakronk suggested.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <blockquote class="source-quote">
                    <div class="quote-content">
